These interactions can enhance binding affinity and selectivity, particularly in systems where traditional hydrogen bonding is less effective. Together, hydrogen bonds and anion-π interactions enable the precise and reversible assembly of host-guest complexes, underpinning many applications in molecular recognition, sensing, and catalysis
